{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01XyaweZNHQYwHmA7Qs5iUW5","type":"tool_result","content":"{\"content\":\"1: #pragma once\\n2: \\n3: #include <cstdint>\\n4: #include <functional>\\n5: #include <memory>\\n6: #include <string>\\n7: \\n8: #include \\\"envoy/access_log/access_log.h\\\"\\n9: #include \\\"envoy/buffer/buffer.h\\\"\\n10: #include \\\"envoy/common/scope_tracker.h\\\"\\n11: #include \\\"envoy/event/dispatcher.h\\\"\\n12: #include \\\"envoy/grpc/status.h\\\"\\n13: #include \\\"envoy/http/codec.h\\\"\\n14: #include \\\"envoy/http/filter_factory.h\\\"\\n15: #include \\\"envoy/http/header_map.h\\\"\\n16: #include \\\"envoy/matcher/matcher.h\\\"\\n17: #include \\\"envoy/router/router.h\\\"\\n18: #include \\\"envoy/router/scopes.h\\\"\\n19: #include \\\"envoy/ssl/connection.h\\\"\\n20: #include \\\"envoy/tracing/tracer.h\\\"\\n21: #include \\\"envoy/upstream/load_balancer.h\\\"\\n22: #include \\\"envoy/upstream/upstream.h\\\"\\n23: \\n24: #include \\\"source/common/common/scope_tracked_object_stack.h\\\"\\n25: \\n26: #include \\\"absl/types/optional.h\\\"\\n27: \\n28: namespace Envoy {\\n29: namespace Router {\\n30: class RouteConfigProvider;\\n31: }\\n32: namespace Http {\\n33: \\n34: /**\\n35:  * Return codes for encode/decode headers filter invocations. The connection manager bases further\\n36:  * filter invocations on the return code of the previous filter.\\n37:  */\\n38: enum class FilterHeadersStatus {\\n39:   // Continue filter chain iteration.\\n40:   Continue,\\n41:   // Do not iterate for headers on any of the remaining filters in the chain.\\n42:   //\\n43:   // Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from decodeData()/encodeData() or calling\\n44:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\\n45:   //\\n46:   // Note that if a local reply was sent, no further iteration for headers as well as data and\\n47:   // trailers for the current filter and the filters following will happen. A local reply can be\\n48:   // triggered via sendLocalReply() or encodeHeaders().\\n49:   StopIteration,\\n50:   // Continue headers iteration to remaining filters, but delay ending the stream. This status MUST\\n51:   // NOT be returned when end_stream is already set to false.\\n52:   //\\n53:   // Used when a filter wants to add a body to a headers-only request/response, but this body is not\\n54:   // readily available. Delaying end_stream allows the filter to add the body once it's available\\n55:   // without stopping headers iteration.\\n56:   //\\n57:   // The filter is responsible to continue the stream by providing a body through calling\\n58:   // injectDecodedDataToFilterChain()/injectEncodedDataToFilterChain(), possibly multiple times\\n59:   // if the body needs to be divided into several chunks. The filter may need to handle\\n60:   // watermark events when injecting a body, see:\\n61:   // https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/blob/main/source/docs/flow_control.md.\\n62:   //\\n63:   // The last call to inject data MUST have end_stream set to true to conclude the stream.\\n64:   // If the filter cannot provide a body the stream should be reset.\\n65:   //\\n66:   // Adding a body through calling addDecodedData()/addEncodedData() then\\n67:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() is currently NOT supported and causes an assert failure.\\n68:   //\\n69:   // Adding trailers in this scenario is currently NOT supported.\\n70:   //\\n71:   // The filter MUST NOT attempt to continue the stream without providing a body using\\n72:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding().\\n73:   //\\n74:   // TODO(yosrym93): Support adding a body in this case by calling addDecodedData()/addEncodedData()\\n75:   // then continueDecoding()/continueEncoding(). To support this a new FilterManager::IterationState\\n76:   // needs to be added and set when a filter returns this status in\\n77:   // FilterManager::decodeHeaders/FilterManager::encodeHeaders()\\n78:   // Currently, when a filter returns this, the IterationState is Continue. This causes ASSERTs in\\n79:   // FilterManager::commonContinue() to fail when continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() is called;\\n80:   // due to trying to continue iteration when the IterationState is already Continue.\\n81:   // In this case, a different ASSERT will be needed to make sure the filter does not try to\\n82:   // continue without adding a body first.\\n83:   //\\n84:   // TODO(yosrym93): Support adding trailers in this case by implementing new functions to inject\\n85:   // trailers, similar to the inject data functions.\\n86:   ContinueAndDontEndStream,\\n87:   // Do not iterate for headers as well as data and trailers for the current filter and the filters\\n88:   // following, and buffer body data for later dispatching. ContinueDecoding() MUST\\n89:   // be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\\n90:   //\\n91:   // Used when a filter wants to stop iteration on data and trailers while waiting for headers'\\n92:   // iteration to resume.\\n93:   //\\n94:   // If buffering the request causes buffered data to exceed the configured buffer limit, a 413 will\\n95:   // be sent to the user. It calls `FilterManager::decodeHeaders()` to start filter chain iteration\\n3. The FilterManager iterates through decoder filters in order, calling their decode methods\\n4.
